<user_id>105302723488545660344<//user_id><user_name>Jon Dale<//user_name><date>1622580921652< /date>< rate>
5< /rate>
< review>
Bottom line up front: the lumber price boom seems to have had little impact on this business, as the pieces I bought today were in the same realm as pieces purchased several months earlier.

They have an excellent selection of well-labeled hardwoods, slabs, and construction materials. They also offer several brands of tools, notably, Festool.

They do have some Festool products in stock, but are in the same boat as all Festool dealers in regards to shortages, etc.

That said, the sales rep seemed to have a good handle on when products would be in stock, and knew a bit of the "corporate why" as to the reason behind tool shortages.

Overall, they were friendly, knowledgeable, and offered more than competitive pricing on all products.<//review>

< Text>
Great customer service and by far the largest selection of lumber in San Diego. Great selection of rare and specialty woods at fair prices. I purchased some beautiful figured maple from them, and I have yet to find anywhere else that carries such beautiful wood.

This is a great place to do a workout on stairs, 292 steps. Everybody is friendly and it feels nice and safe at least during the day. I understand there used to be some noise and other problems at night so it closes one hour after dusk and opens one hour before sunrise.

My first time I walked it up-and-down (up and down counted as one time) 4 times at a leisurely pace and it took about half an hour. I talk to others who were doing it 6 to 12 times. My legs felt a bit wobbly right after, but I'm not to sure now. A good start! :-)<//text>
